# Phase B Module Truth Map

Date: 2026-07-09
Branch: master
Latest commit at scout: 44bbb30 phase A structural validation gate

## Verdict

- B1 Every module classified: PASS (399 modules; WIRED=292, BLOCKED=96, PRESERVED-DEAD=10, REJECTED-PRESERVED=1).
- B2 No silent module: PASS (0 roleless rows found).
- B3 Seven authorities named and duplicates surfaced: PASS (7 owners named; 9 duplicate/conflict seams listed for Phase C).

## Scope

- Inventory scope includes 399 code/operator modules: Python source/tests, PowerShell/VBS launch/audit scripts, operator UI runtime assets, and control/mode.txt.
- Docs, reports, README/governance packets, requirements, pytest.ini, state, logs, data DBs, venv, and secret/runtime folders are evidence/config/runtime artifacts, not source modules, and are not row-classified.
- This is a static truth map using imports, text references, markers, and Phase A proof. It is not a live PAPER run and does not prove broker runtime behavior.

## Classification Definitions

- WIRED: importable/runnable and holding a lawful role as runtime, operator, contract, UI, script, or proof module.
- BLOCKED: should contribute value but cannot truthfully be treated as complete runtime wiring; blocker and integration plan named.
- PRESERVED-DEAD: intentionally inactive or shadowed reference/quarantine/tombstone with named reason.
- REJECTED-PRESERVED: explicitly rejected duplicate authority retained only for reference.
